I guess groupId/artifactId should remain unchanged here, because mock-javamail still has a dependency on the old version: https://repo1.maven.org/maven2/org/jvnet/mock-javamail/mock-javamail/1.7/mock-javamail-1.7.pom

Pascal

afaik its our own bundle for mock testing in osgi - we dont use that external jar but mock javax mail itself.

Ah darn there is other components using the old mvn name - why the hell did they change it to com.sun - that company is no longer!.

Do you mind doing a PR to fix the remainder?

You can find the problems with
find . -name 'pom.xml' | xargs grep "javax.mail"

Np, I will create a PR.

I should really have searched for other usages when creating the first PR. Sorry!

No problem we like to get PRs and keep the libraries up to date - there is 200+ components so plenty of work ;)

As I understand it you rebundle a shaded version of mock-javamail. The pom (`org.apache.camel.tests.mock-javamail_1.7-2.17-SNAPSHOT.pom`) now includes these dependencies:

```
<dependency>
  <groupId>javax.mail</groupId>
  <artifactId>mail</artifactId>
  <version>1.4</version>
  <scope>compile</scope>
</dependency>
...
<dependency>
  <groupId>com.sun.mail</groupId>
  <artifactId>javax.mail</artifactId>
  <version>1.5.5</version>
  <scope>compile</scope>
</dependency>
```

that isn't correct I think.
